I did not give a bad review because the hotel environment was good, the air was good, and the service of the room aunt was good.
Let me talk about the experience when I checked in first! The front desk receptionist answered one question after another, and did not actively ask about the customer's needs. You have to look at her face. The current service industry is very competitive. I really can't see how this hotel is managed and how to train employees.
No one greeted me during the stay. Since I took a plane and a taxi early in the morning, the elderly and children were very tired. I ordered takeout directly at the hotel and took a break. The takeout arrived. I asked three people and finally walked to the gate security to tell me the exact location of the takeout. From the front desk to the concierge, they were all cold and ignored the feelings of the guests. After all, it should be a four-star hotel! Don't they have the most basic etiquette? Let's talk about the room. The first time the phone was broken, I could only + the hotel's official WeChat or go to the front desk. After reporting the repair, the room attendant solved it. The hands-free button was available, but there was no sound in the receiver. Doesn't such a big hotel have an engineering depar**ent? The next day, the TV didn't turn on again!
I would like to thank the housekeeper that night. When the kid accidentally knocked over the water cup and the bed sheet got wet, the housekeeper ran back and forth twice to change the bedding. Although it is her essential job, I would like to thank the employee again for the inconvenience.
The next day, the lobby manager checked me out and asked about my stay experience. I told her the truth. The other party said that in order to show her sincerity, she would give me a free upgrade next time I stay. I refused directly. First of all, you don't know the purpose of my stay, how can you know that I will come to Jieyang next time? Since some issues were not proactively contacted and resolved on the same day, but were casually mentioned when checking out, there was no sincerity at all. Do you think you will choose this hotel next time?

msg:On the eve of the Spring Festival, I suddenly decided to visit Chaoshan
But seeing that everyone seems to be coming, the hotel prices have increased many times.
I definitely wouldn't choose this. It's not cost-effective.
So after checking a small book, I decided to focus on Jieyang.
Because I drive myself, it doesn‚Äôt matter even if I‚Äôm not in the city center.
Jieyang Yingbin Hotel did not hesitate to choose the side of the mountain. The air is good and it is also clean.
The hotel is like a garden-style hotel. It is very comfortable and surrounded by green trees. It is still very big when you go around.
There are two swimming pools, which are quite large and occupy the courtyards on the left and right sides. Unfortunately, they are not open for use in the summer.
The check-in staff also provided very good and professional service.
After entering the room, the room staff also brought a fruit plate, which was very comfortable.
The bed in the room is 1.35 meters long and very comfortable. Charging is very convenient.
In the hotel, there is a Weilai charging station on the right hand side after entering the gate. Fast charging is available but not open. Slow charging is 0.91 yuan per kilowatt hour. The price is quite good.
There are other brands of charging piles outside the hotel gate on both sides. The price is cheaper than NIO and there are fast and slow charging. When we stay in the hotel, we definitely choose slow charging. It is very convenient.
It‚Äôs very convenient to eat nearby if you drive

Those who can be called "guesthouses" are naturally not ordinary people, but this one is obviously an exception.

I booked a superior double room, but there was no welcome guide or help with luggage at the hotel, and there was no room type upgrade at the front desk. I asked how much I need to pay to upgrade to the next room type, and the reply was 300. I took a look and decided that it was only 200 more expensive. to, so give up.

The front desk said that they would arrange a room with a good view for me. I was stunned when I entered the room. It is true that there is a balcony, and it is true that the balcony faces the mountain, but this is not a blindfold. I can't see Mount Tai, it is a blindfold! Is this what is called "the view is good"?

The room is 40 square meters, and it looks relatively clean, but the carpet is too dirty to the naked eye. Equipped with a Chinese tea set, a few bags of Lipton tea bags were given, and the mattress was very hard.

The bathroom has a single basin and a bathtub, but the length is not too shallow. I can't bury my stomach when I lie down. I use the hotel's own canned accessories. Fortunately, I have Oulong, so I didn't dare to use it.

What makes me feel strange is that the price of the room items is correct, but the bath salts also need to be paid for, a pack of 10 yuan, and almost unlimited supply in other five-star hotels. I didn't bring my own before leaving, sorry.

The toilet is too high and uncomfortable, and the shower head is directly broken and cannot be used.

The most strange thing is that when I checked out, I found that the room card could not be found, and the hotel directly deducted 50 yuan, which is unique in the five-star hotels I have stayed in! And there is no sign anywhere, or when you check in, you will be informed that you will be compensated for 50 yuan for the loss of the room card?

How much does the room card cost for your hotel? Dare to come up with a list of details as a basis for fines?

This alone is enough to block it.
